# Test source

```ts
  1  | import { expect, test } from "@playwright/test";
  2  | import { loginAsAdmin } from "./helpers/auth";
  3  | 
  4  | const ROUTES: { path: string; expectText?: RegExp | string }[] = [
  5  |   { path: "/", expectText: /Dashboard|Today|Activity/i },
  6  |   { path: "/customers", expectText: /Customers|Clients/i },
  7  |   { path: "/boarding", expectText: /Boarding/i },
  8  |   { path: "/daycare", expectText: /Daycare/i },
  9  |   { path: "/grooming", expectText: /Grooming/i },
  10 |   { path: "/billing", expectText: /Billing/i },
  11 |   { path: "/billing/invoices", expectText: /Invoices/i },
  12 |   { path: "/billing/invoices/new", expectText: /Invoice|Create/i },
  13 |   { path: "/staff", expectText: /Staff/i },
  14 |   { path: "/profile", expectText: /Profile/i },
  15 |   { path: "/settings", expectText: /Settings/i },
  16 |   { path: "/settings/vets", expectText: /Vet/i },
  17 |   { path: "/settings/rooms", expectText: /Room/i },
  18 |   { path: "/agent", expectText: /Agent/i },
  19 |   { path: "/dashboard/checkins", expectText: /Check-?in/i },
  20 |   { path: "/customers?filter=low-wallet" },
  21 |   { path: "/billing/invoices?status=overdue" },
  22 |   { path: "/boarding?date=today&view=check-ins" },
  23 |   { path: "/grooming?date=today" },
  24 |   { path: "/daycare?tab=operations" },
  25 | ];
  26 | 
  27 | test.describe("route-smoke", () => {
  28 |   test.use({ storageState: { cookies: [], origins: [] } });
  29 | 
  30 |   test("logged-out user is redirected to login", async ({ page }) => {
  31 |     await page.goto("/");
  32 |     await expect(page).toHaveURL(/\/login/);
  33 |   });
  34 | 
  35 |   test.describe("authenticated", () => {
  36 |     test.use({ storageState: "tests/e2e/.auth/admin.json" });
  37 | 
  38 |   test("all main routes load without runtime errors", async ({ page }) => {
  39 |     const consoleErrors: string[] = [];
  40 |     page.on("console", (msg) => {
  41 |       if (msg.type() === "error") {
  42 |         const text = msg.text();
  43 |         if (/favicon|404.*\.(png|ico|svg)/i.test(text)) return;
  44 |         // Dev-only debug canary (App.tsx / SetupPasswordPage) — not a product defect.
  45 |         if (/7457\/ingest|ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED/i.test(text)) return;
  46 |         consoleErrors.push(text);
  47 |       }
  48 |     });
  49 |     page.on("pageerror", (err) => {
  50 |       consoleErrors.push(`pageerror: ${err.message}`);
  51 |     });
  52 | 
  53 |     await loginAsAdmin(page);
  54 | 
  55 |     for (const route of ROUTES) {
  56 |       consoleErrors.length = 0;
  57 |       await page.goto(route.path);
  58 |       await page.waitForLoadState("networkidle");
  59 |       await expect(page.locator("body")).not.toContainText("Unexpected Application Error");
  60 |       await expect(page.locator("body")).not.toContainText("Something went wrong");
  61 |       if (route.expectText) {
> 62 |         await expect(page.locator("main").first()).toContainText(route.expectText);
     |                                                    ^ Error: expect(locator).toContainText(expected) failed
  63 |       }
  64 |       expect(
  65 |         consoleErrors,
  66 |         `console errors on ${route.path}: ${consoleErrors.join("; ")}`,
  67 |       ).toEqual([]);
  68 |     }
  69 |   });
  70 | 
  71 |   test("removed park route returns not found", async ({ page }) => {
  72 |     await loginAsAdmin(page);
  73 |     await page.goto("/park");
  74 |     await page.waitForLoadState("networkidle");
  75 |     await expect(page.locator("body")).toContainText(/not found|404/i);
  76 |   });
  77 |   });
  78 | });
  79 | 
```
